< Review>
From the outside you wouldn't expect a good place, but it turns out the pizza is pretty good here. It's kinda cramped inside, but there's indoor and outdoor seating. Pricing is fine, there's a good selection of slices, but you can also get sandwiches or salads or pasta. I opted for the margherita and the spinach/ricotta...both were good, I wish they were a little warmer, but there was flavor, sufficient toppings, and the crust was crispy and chewy.</Review>

<user_name>Joan Brent< /user_name><Time>1572206131236< /Time>< Rate>
1</Rate>
< text>
We placed an online order for an associate's birthday at our office downtown Friday, Oct. 25th.  A Brooklyn Pizzeria downtown was the Birthday Girl's choice as she is a vegetarian.  These comments are not meant for A Brooklyn Pizzeria directly.  They are to caution any customer who chooses to order online.  After the order did not arrive on time, we contacted the restaurant to check on the status of our order.  A Brooklyn Pizzeria never received our order.  After researching the situation, we learned their online ordering is handled by "Menu Star Food Ordering" not Grub Hub as advertised. Beware restaurants and customers.  There is no connection from this company to the restaurants they represent for online delivering.  We reordered by telephone directly through A Brooklyn Pizzeria.  Our order arrived in a timely manner.  Even though an 1/2 hour late, the Birthday gathering did happen and the food was great.  However, Menu Star Food Ordering had made one attempt to be paid but it did not go through my associate's credit card.  The bottom line, A Brooklyn Pizzeria's staff and food are authentic.  Don't trust the online ordering process.  Beware of Menu Star Food Ordering !!</text>

< text>
This is such an awesome place just because it's a hut in the middle of a parking lot with plenty of shaded seating. It's also pretty cheap food for decent cheap Chinese food. They even take credit card!

What I like about the menu is that most items are about the same price, so you can really just choose what you want to eat. I got the chicken with broccoli, which came with either rice of fried rice. I opted for the latter. The portion is decent and I was satisfied at the end of the meal. The carryout is well-packaged and nothing spilled.

I think the only issue is that it took about 10 minutes to get my food, which is a bit long, but not too bad.<//text>

< Name>
Star Traveler< /Name>
<time>1541718902268</time><Rate>2</Rate>< Review>
It's fair to say that this place is a 'good deal' if you relate the quantity of food to the price.  However, I find the food here bland and without character, largely because of inadequate seasoning.  Also notable is that they use exclusively American vegetables (corn, mushrooms, carrots, green pepper, celery, broccoli) that are nearly the same in every dish.  You will not find any Chinese vegetables like water chestnuts, bok choy, bamboo shoots, bean sprouts, etc. being used here.  The result is rather unimpressive Chinese food that is not really Chinese food!<//Review>

<Text>I would call this place a hole in the wall, but that wouldn't be entirely accurate. It's more like hole in the street--you can see it from afar, but you don't pay much mind to it and instinctively avoid it. There isn't much signage, and it is very unassuming in that old donut shop way.

That however has no bearing on the type of food that comes out of here, however. The tastiest egg rolls (and large, too), the most flavorful Mongolian beef, and the kung Pao chicken exist here. Definitely something to check out.<//Text>< Pictures>

This place gives the least amount of meat possible to be considered a sandwich.  I ordered the Philly cheesesteak with grilled onions and cheese, since that's what the place was known for, the sandwich maybe had 2oz. of meat, the rest was onion and cheese, I went there based on the reviews and pictures.  I received about one eighth of the meat that the pictures show.  All I could taste was onion and cheese. Their regular cheesesteak comes with mushrooms andbell peppers, obviously that's a bunch of inexpensive fluff.  My daughter ordered a ham sandwich it came with two thin slices of ham and one slice of cheese...
Over priced and overrated.
This was my first and last time. Service was slow also...< /text>

<Review>Drove two hours just to get to this beach because of how wonderful my first experience was when I stayed at the Embassy Suites Mandalay Beach Resort. Had an ocean view room and remembered how beautiful, clean, and quiet this beach was. Albeit, this second time there were more people which is expected for Labor Day weekend. Definitely still quiet and clean regardless.
-Room enough for everyone to have their personal space.
-Love that it's dog friendly (if you leash and pick up their poop of course) when we brought a chihuahua and weimeraner.
-Security drives around periodically to enforce rules which is comforting.
-Bathrooms could be cleaner but I've seen worse.
-Concrete and plastic paths leading to the beach which is great for coolers and feet.
-Waves aren't big so my short self doesn't get swept away.
Definitely recommend this beach to those who are tired of other packed and dirty SoCal beaches!</Review></record></dataset><record>
